              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>Static variables are <a href="./Variable (Computer Science)">variables</a> in which the <a href="./Compiler">compiler</a> allocates memory for them throughout the entire run of the program. Static variables are placed on the <a href="./Memory#Data Segment">data segment</a> of a programs <a href="./Memory">memory</a> and are usually associated before the program is executed.</p>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Endianness
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>Endianness refers to the direction in which <a href="./Byte">bytes</a> are transmitted over a data communication method.</p>

          <div class="col-md">
            <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<h1>Little-Endian</h1>
<p>Little-endian works by transmitting / storing the least significant byte first.</p>

          </div>
        
          </div>
        <h2>Example</h2>
<p>Consider the number <code>0x12345678</code> if we were to write this to memory at the index <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D456 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container>, we would get the following memory values:</p>

<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Byte Extension
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>Byte extension describes the process by which <a href="./Byte">bytes</a> are added when a stored values <a href="./Memory">memory</a> size needs to be increased (ie. from a <a href="./Byte">byte</a> to an int). There are two types of byte extension <strong>Signed Extension</strong> and <strong>Zero Extension</strong>. Both methods of byte extensions pad the start of the value instead of the end.</p>
<h1>Signed Extension</h1>
<p>Signed extension extends the <a href="./Byte">bytes</a>, with whatever the sign of the data is, (for example -11, would be padded with 1's and 11 would be padded would 0's). In <a href="./C">C</a> signed extension is used for all signed data types.</p>
<h2>Example</h2>

class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr></mjx-itable></mjx-table></mjx-mtable></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<h1>Zero Extension</h1>
<p>Zero extension extends the <a href="./Byte">bytes</a>, with zeroes, no matter what the sign of the data is. In <a href="./C">C</a> zero extension is used for all unsigned data types.</p>
<h2>Example</h2>

padding-left: 1em; padding-right: 0; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0; padding-top: 0.15em;"><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0; padding-right: 1em; padding-top: 0.15em;"><mjx-mtext class="mjx-ty"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D69E TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D697 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D69C TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D692 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D690 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D697 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D68E TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D68D TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c20 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D692 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D697 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D69D TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c20 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D68C TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c20 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c20 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D68B TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c3B TEX-T"></mjx-c></mjx-mtext><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-left: 1em; padding-right: 0; padding-top: 0.15em;"><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0; padding-top: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mstyle style="color: #61afef;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr></mjx-itable></mjx-table></mjx-mtable></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Byte Truncation
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>Byte extension describes the process by which <a href="./Byte">bytes</a> are removed when a stored values <a href="./Memory">memory</a> size needs to be decrease (ie. from an int to a byte). Bits are always removed from the start of the value called truncation.</p>
<h1>Example</h1>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mtable style="min-width: 27.905em;"><mjx-table><mjx-itable><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0; padding-right: 1em; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-mtext class="mjx-ty"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D692 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D697 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D69D TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c20 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D68B TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c20 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c20 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c2D TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D7FC TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c3B TEX-T"></mjx-c></mjx-mtext><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-left: 1em; padding-right: 0; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mstyle style="color: #61afef;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0; padding-top: 0.15em;"><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0; padding-right: 1em; padding-top: 0.15em;"><mjx-mtext class="mjx-ty"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D68C TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D691 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D68A TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D69B TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c20 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D68C TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c20 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c20 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c28 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D68C TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D691 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D68A TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D69B TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c29 TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D68B TEX-T"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c3B TEX-T"></mjx-c></mjx-mtext><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-left: 1em; padding-right: 0; padding-top: 0.15em;"><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0; padding-top: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mstyle style="color: #e06c75;"><mjx-menclose><mjx-box style="padding: 0.267em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle></mjx-box><mjx-ustrike style="width: 11.984em; transform: rotate(-0.1rad) translateY(0.0335em);"></mjx-ustrike></mjx-menclose></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr></mjx-itable></mjx-table></mjx-mtable></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Memory
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<h1>Accessing Memory</h1>
<p>Memory can be accessed by the <a href="./Central Processing Unit">CPU</a>, and must be accessed in contiguous, power of two size chunks of <a href="./Byte">bytes</a>.</p>
<h1>Areas of Memory</h1>
<p>The memory of a computer is usually split up into 4 main sections.</p>
<h2>Code Segment</h2>
<p>The <strong>code segment</strong> contains the compiled <a href="./Machine Instructions">machine instructions</a> and is read only to ensure you can't accidentally overwrite your code at runtime.</p>
<h2>Data Segment</h2>
<p>The <strong>data segment</strong> contains any <a href="./Global Variable">global</a> and <a href="./Static Variable">static variables</a>.</p>
<h2>Stack</h2>
<p>The <strong>stack</strong> stores <a href="./Local Variable">local variables</a>, <a href="./Function Parameter">function parameters</a>, and <a href="./Return Address">return addresses</a>. The stack typically grows downward towards lower <a href="./Memory Address">addresses</a> in memory and is automatically managed, (ie. the <a href="./Memory Address">addresses</a> are freed when functions return).</p>
<h2>Heap</h2>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Heap Memory
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>The <strong>heap</strong> is used for <a href="./Dynamically Allocated Memory">dynamically allocated memory</a> (ie. <code>malloc</code> in <a href="./C">C</a> and <code>new</code> in <a href="./C++">C++</a>). The <strong>heap</strong> typically grows upwards towards higher addresses in memory and is manually managed, (ie. you must free the memory when you're done with it).</p>
<h1>Pitfalls</h1>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Dangling Pointers
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>When a program accesses memory that has already been freed, the contents at that location are <strong>undefined</strong> because the system may have reallocated that memory for other purposes. <a href="./Pointer">Pointers</a> pointing to this freed memory are called <strong>dangling pointers</strong>.</p>
<h1>Example</h1>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">int</span> *i = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-type">int</span>;
*i = <span class="hljs-number">5</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">delete</span> i;

cout &lt;&lt; *i &lt;&lt; endl;
</code></pre><p>Here, <code>i</code> <a href="./Pointer">points</a> to memory that has been deallocated. Accessing or writing to it can produce unexpected results.</p>
<h1>Avoiding Dangling Pointers</h1>
<p>To prevent using freed memory, you can set the <a href="./Pointer">pointer</a> to <a href="./Memory Address#NULL Address">NULL</a> after deletion. This way, dereferencing it will trigger a crash (e.g., segmentation fault), making the bug easier to detect:</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">int</span> *i = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-type">int</span>;
*i = <span class="hljs-number">5</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">delete</span> i;
i = <span class="hljs-literal">NULL</span>;

cout &lt;&lt; *i &lt;&lt; endl; <span class="hljs-comment">// Seg fault</span>
</code></pre>
              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Memory Leak
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>When a program loses access to allocated space before it has been freed (ie. by reassigning a <a href="./Pointer">pointer</a>), the space can no loner be referenced, or freed. This memory therefore remains marked as allocated for the lifetime of the program. Typically memory leaks occur with memory on the <a href="./Heap Memory">heap</a>.</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">int</span> *i = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-type">int</span>;
<span class="hljs-type">int</span> b = <span class="hljs-number">2</span>

*i = <span class="hljs-number">5</span>;
i = &amp;b;
</code></pre><blockquote>
<p>The original address of <code>i</code> was lost and can no longer be freed causing a memory leak</p>
</blockquote>

              </div>
            </div></p>

              </div>
            </div></p>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Memory Address
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>A memory address describes the location in <a href="./Memory">memory</a> where a given variable or identifier stores data.</p>
<h1>Special Addresses</h1>
<h2>NULL Address</h2>
<p>The null address is <code>0x0000</code> and represents an empty value. Trying to dereference this address with throw an error as it doesn't exist.</p>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Pointer
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>A pointer is a <a href="./Variable">variable</a> which stores a <a href="./Memory Address">memory address</a>.</p>
<h1>Declaring Pointer Variables</h1>
<h2><a href="./C">C</a> and <a href="./C++">C++</a></h2>
<p>Pointer variables are defined as follows:</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">int</span> *ptr;
</code></pre><p>where <code>int</code> can be any data type and defines the type of value at that pointers <a href="./Memory Address">address</a>. Additionally <code>ptr</code> is just the name of the variable and can be any valid name.</p>
<h1>Pointer Operations</h1>
<h2><a href="./C">C</a> and <a href="./C++">C++</a></h2>
<h3>Address Operator</h3>
<p>The address operator gets the <a href="./Memory Address">address</a> of an existing variable and is expressed by placing a <code>&amp;</code> before the variable.</p>
<h4>Example</h4>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">int</span> x = <span class="hljs-number">23</span>;
<span class="hljs-type">int</span> *p = &amp;x;
</code></pre><p>The variable <code>p</code> now stores the <a href="./Memory Address">address</a> of <code>x</code>.</p>
<h3>Dereferencing Operator</h3>
<p>The Dereferencing operator gets value at an <a href="./Memory Address">address</a> is expressed by placing a <code>*</code> before the pointer.</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">int</span> x = <span class="hljs-number">23</span>;
<span class="hljs-type">int</span> *p = &amp;x;

*p = <span class="hljs-number">50</span>;
cout &lt;&lt; x &lt;&lt; endl; <span class="hljs-comment">// Outputs 50</span>
</code></pre><h1><a href="./C++">C++</a></h1>
<h3><code>new</code> Keyword</h3>
<p>The <code>new</code> keyword allocates new space on the <a href="./Heap Memory">heap</a> and returns the first <a href="./Memory Address">address</a> of the allocated space.</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">int</span> *b = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-type">int</span>;
</code></pre><h3><code>delete</code> Keyword</h3>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">int</span> *b = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-type">int</span>;
*b = <span class="hljs-number">2</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">delete</span> b;
</code></pre><p>For arrays allocated on the heap the <code>delete[]</code> keyword can be used</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">int</span> *b = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-type">int</span>[<span class="hljs-number">3</span>]{<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>};

<span class="hljs-keyword">delete</span>[] b;
</code></pre><p>The <code>delete</code> keyword releases the memory at the <a href="./Memory Address">address</a> referenced by the pointer variable passed to it.</p>
<h1>Stacking Pointers</h1>
<p>Because pointers can &quot;point&quot; to any <a href="./Memory Address">address</a> in <a href="./Memory">memory</a> we can create pointers to pointers</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">int</span> x = <span class="hljs-number">5</span>;
<span class="hljs-type">int</span>* p = &amp;x;          <span class="hljs-comment">// Memory address of `x`</span>
<span class="hljs-type">int</span>** q = &amp;p;         <span class="hljs-comment">// Memory address of `p`</span>
<span class="hljs-type">int</span>*** r = &amp;q;        <span class="hljs-comment">// Memory address of `r`</span>

cout &lt;&lt; **r &lt;&lt; endl;  <span class="hljs-comment">// Memory address of `x` (value of `p)</span>
cout &lt;&lt; **q &lt;&lt; endl;  <span class="hljs-comment">// Value of `x`</span>
cout &lt;&lt; ***r &lt;&lt; endl; <span class="hljs-comment">// Value of `x`</span>
</code></pre>
              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Address Alignment
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>Address alignment describes the process by which <a href="./Memory Address">addresses</a> are allocated such that they are multiples of the object's size. Aligned addresses are faster to access on most <a href="./Central Processing Unit">CPU's</a> and on some unaligned addresses are not supported.</p>
<h1><a href="./Structure">Structure</a> Alignment</h1>
<p><a href="./Structure">Structures</a> are aligned differently to basic <a href="./Data Type">data types</a> as they are composites, their alignment follows the following 3 rules:</p>
<ol>
<li>Fields of primitive types are aligned according to their size.</li>
<li>Fields whose types are <a href="./Structure">structures</a> or <a href="./Array">arrays</a> are aligned to the largest of their fields’ alignments</li>
<li>The size of a <a href="./Structure">structure</a> must be a multiple of its alignment</li>
</ol>
<p>When padding is introduced it must always be added between or after fields, ensuring that the alignment of the field before the padding is maintained.</p>
<h2>Examples</h2>
<h3>Example 1</h3>
<p>Given the following struct determine the offset of <code>b</code> as well as the total size of the struct and the alignment</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-class"><span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> <span class="hljs-title">ExampleOne</span> {</span>
    <span class="hljs-type">char</span>  a;
    <span class="hljs-type">int</span>   b;
    <span class="hljs-type">short</span> c;
};
</code></pre><p>The individual fields have sizes of 1, 4, and 2 bytes respectively meaning the overall alignment of the struct must be 4 bytes, the size of the fields in the struct total to 7 bytes, meaning it must be padded up to 12 bytes, we can do this by adding padding of 3 bytes to <code>a</code> and 4 bytes to the end of <code>c</code>.</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Size (Bytes)</th>
<th>Offset</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>char a;</code></td>
<td>1</td>
<td>0</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>padding</td>
<td>3</td>
<td></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>int b;</code></td>
<td>4</td>
<td>4</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>short c;</code></td>
<td>2</td>
<td>6</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>padding</td>
<td>4</td>
<td></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td></td>
<td><strong>Total:</strong> 12</td>
<td></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Reference Counting
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>Reference counting is a method of managing <a href="./Memory">memory</a> to decrease the risks common memory pitfalls like <a href="./Memory Leak">memory leaks</a> or <a href="./Dangling Pointers">dangling pointers</a>. Reference counting follows 4 basic rules to perform this</p>
<ol>
<li>Initialize the reference count to <strong>one</strong> (as the caller has a reference)</li>
<li>Any <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a> that stores a reference <strong>increments</strong> the count</li>
<li>Any <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a> that discards a reference <strong>decrements</strong> the count</li>
<li>Never free an object directly, instead the object is free when the count goes to <strong>zero</strong></li>
</ol>
<h1>General Examples</h1>
<h2>When a Reference is a Parameter</h2>
<p>When a reference is passed to a <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a> as a parameter, the caller necessarily must maintain it for the duration of the call so the callee doesn't need to call <code>keep_ref</code>, <strong>unless</strong> the callee saves the pointer somewhere that will outlast the call (ie. a global variable), or the callee returns the pointer to the caller.</p>
<h2>When a Reference is a Return Value</h2>
<p>When a reference is returned from a <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a>, the callee must have a reference to the value which it returns to the caller, when it returns it though it transfers that reference to the caller, it's then the callers responsibility to call <code>free_ref</code> when it no longer needs the reference.</p>
<h2>When a Reference is Stored in a Local Variable</h2>
<p>References' stored in local variables necessarily must go away when the <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a> returns so the <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a> must call <code>free_ref</code> before it returns.</p>
<h1>Implementations</h1>
<h2>Concrete Type</h2>
<p>If the struct you're reference counting has a concrete type reference counting can be implemented as follows:</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> buffer *<span class="hljs-title function_">rc_malloc</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {
	<span class="hljs-class"><span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> <span class="hljs-title">buffer</span> *<span class="hljs-title">buf</span> =</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">malloc</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> buffer));
	buf-&gt;ref_count = <span class="hljs-number">1</span>;

	<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> buf;
}

<span class="hljs-type">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">rc_keep_ref</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> buffer *buf)</span> {
	buf-&gt;ref_count++;
}

<span class="hljs-type">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">rc_free_ref</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> buffer *buf)</span> {
	buf-&gt;ref_count--;
	
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (buf-&gt;ref_count == <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) <span class="hljs-built_in">free</span>(buf);
}
</code></pre><h2>General Type</h2>
<p>A more general method can be used which works for any input type, this is done by reserving 8 bytes before the actual allocated memory for the ref count.</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">void</span>* <span class="hljs-title function_">rc_malloc</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-type">int</span> num_bytes)</span> {
	<span class="hljs-comment">// Add 8 bytes to store the ref_count</span>
	<span class="hljs-type">int</span> *ref_count = <span class="hljs-built_in">malloc</span>(n+<span class="hljs-number">8</span>);
	*ref_count = <span class="hljs-number">1</span>;
	
	<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> ((<span class="hljs-type">void</span>*) ref_count) + <span class="hljs-number">8</span>;
}

<span class="hljs-type">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">rc_keep_ref</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-type">void</span>* ptr)</span> {
	<span class="hljs-type">int</span> *ref_count = ptr - <span class="hljs-number">8</span>;
	(*ref_count)++;
}

<span class="hljs-type">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">rc_free_ref</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-type">void</span>* ptr)</span> {
	<span class="hljs-type">int</span> *ref_count = ptr - <span class="hljs-number">8</span>;
	(*ref_count)--;
	
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (*ref_count == <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) <span class="hljs-built_in">free</span>(ref_count);
}
</code></pre>
              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Conditional (Computer Science)
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>A conditional is a type of <a href="./Control Flow">control flow</a> that branches based on one or more expressions.</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">int</span> a;
<span class="hljs-built_in">scanf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;%d&quot;</span>, &amp;a);

<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (a % <span class="hljs-number">2</span> == <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {
	<span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;%d is even&quot;</span>, a);
} <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
	<span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;%d is odd&quot;</span>, a);
}
</code></pre><blockquote>
<p>Example of a conditional statement that checks whether a number is even or odd</p>
</blockquote>
<h1>Low Level Implementation</h1>
<p>At the <a href="./Assembly">assembly</a> level, <strong>conditionals</strong> are implemented using <a href="./Jump Instruction">jumps</a> as well as logic for the condition. The <a href="./Compiler">compiler</a> translates the boolean expression of the condition into arithmetic ones depending on the architecture.</p>
<pre><code>&lt;init&gt;
<span class="hljs-comment">&#x27;conditional setup</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">goto</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">then</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> &lt;condition&gt;
<span class="hljs-symbol">else:</span>
	<span class="hljs-comment">&#x27;alternative body</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">goto</span> end_if
<span class="hljs-symbol">then:</span>
	<span class="hljs-comment">&#x27;consequent body</span>
<span class="hljs-symbol">end_if:</span>
</code></pre><h2>Example</h2>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Conditional (SM213)
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>Given the <a href="./C">C</a> code:</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">int</span> a = <span class="hljs-number">5</span>;
<span class="hljs-type">int</span> b = <span class="hljs-number">2</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (a &gt; b) {
	<span class="hljs-comment">// consequent</span>
} <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
	<span class="hljs-comment">// alternative</span>
}
</code></pre><p>write an equivalent <a href="./Conditional (Computer Science)">conditional</a> in <a href="./SM213 Assembly">assembly</a></p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-keyword">.pos </span><span class="hljs-number">0x1000</span>
	<span class="hljs-comment"># &lt;init&gt;</span>
	<span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> <span class="hljs-variable">$a</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>         <span class="hljs-comment"># r0 = &amp;a</span>
	<span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> (<span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>), <span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>       <span class="hljs-comment"># r0 = a</span>
	<span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> <span class="hljs-variable">$b</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>         <span class="hljs-comment"># r1 = &amp;b</span>
	<span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> (<span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>), <span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>       <span class="hljs-comment"># r1 = b</span>
	
	<span class="hljs-keyword">mv</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r2</span>         <span class="hljs-comment"># r2 = b</span>
	<span class="hljs-keyword">not</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">r2</span>            <span class="hljs-comment"># r2 = !b</span>
	<span class="hljs-keyword">inc</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">r2</span>            <span class="hljs-comment"># r2 = -b</span>
	
	<span class="hljs-keyword">add</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r2</span>        <span class="hljs-comment"># r2 = a-b</span>
	
	<span class="hljs-keyword">bgt</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">r2</span>, then      <span class="hljs-comment"># a-b &gt; 0 =&gt; goto then</span>
	
	<span class="hljs-title function_">else:</span> 
		<span class="hljs-comment"># alternative</span>
		<span class="hljs-keyword">br</span> end_if
	
	<span class="hljs-title function_">then:</span>
		<span class="hljs-comment"># consequent</span>

	<span class="hljs-title function_">end_if:</span> 

<span class="hljs-keyword">.pos </span><span class="hljs-number">0x2000</span>
	<span class="hljs-title function_">a:</span>      <span class="hljs-keyword">.long </span><span class="hljs-number">5</span>
	<span class="hljs-title function_">b:</span>      <span class="hljs-keyword">.long </span><span class="hljs-number">2</span>
</code></pre>
              </div>
            </div></p>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                For Loop
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>A for loop is a type of <a href="./Control Flow">control flow</a> statement that repeatedly runs a section of code until a condition is satisfied.</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (<span class="hljs-type">int</span> i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt; <span class="hljs-number">3</span>; ++i) {
    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;%d&quot;</span>, i);
}
</code></pre><blockquote>
<p>Example of a for loop that prints &quot;012&quot; in <a href="./C">C</a></p>
</blockquote>
<h1>Low Level Implementation</h1>
<p>At the <a href="./Assembly">assembly</a> level, <strong>for loops</strong> are implemented using <strong>conditional and unconditional</strong> <a href="./Jump Instruction">jumps</a>. The <a href="./Compiler">compiler</a> translates the initialization, condition check, increment, and loop body into equivalent jump-based <a href="./Control Flow">control flow</a>.</p>
<pre><code>&lt;init&gt;
<span class="hljs-symbol">loop_start:</span>
    <span class="hljs-comment">&#x27;evaluate condition</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">goto</span> end_loop <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">not</span> &lt;continue_condition&gt;

    <span class="hljs-comment">&#x27;loop body</span>
    ...

    <span class="hljs-comment">&#x27;increment and repeat</span>
    &lt;<span class="hljs-keyword">step</span>&gt;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">goto</span> loop_start
<span class="hljs-symbol">end_loop:</span>
</code></pre><h2>Example</h2>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                For Loop (SM213)
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>Given the <a href="./C">C</a> code:</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (<span class="hljs-type">int</span> i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt; <span class="hljs-number">3</span>; ++i) {
	<span class="hljs-comment">// ...</span>
}
</code></pre><p>write an equivalent <a href="./For Loop">for loop</a> in <a href="./SM213 Assembly">assembly</a></p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-keyword">.pos </span><span class="hljs-number">0x1000</span>
	<span class="hljs-comment"># &lt;init&gt;</span>
	<span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> <span class="hljs-variable">$i</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>         <span class="hljs-comment"># r0 = &amp;i</span>
	<span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> (<span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>), <span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>       <span class="hljs-comment"># r0 = i</span>
	<span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> $<span class="hljs-number">-3</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>        <span class="hljs-comment"># r1 = 3</span>
	
	<span class="hljs-title function_">loop_start:</span> 
		<span class="hljs-keyword">mov</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r2</span>    <span class="hljs-comment"># r2 = i</span>
		<span class="hljs-keyword">add</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r2</span>    <span class="hljs-comment"># r2 = i - 3 (allows us to use beq)</span>
		
		<span class="hljs-comment"># evaluate condition</span>
		<span class="hljs-keyword">beq</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>, end_loop <span class="hljs-comment"># go to just after loop</span>
		
		<span class="hljs-comment"># loop body</span>
		
		<span class="hljs-comment"># increment and repeat</span>
		<span class="hljs-keyword">inc</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>
		<span class="hljs-keyword">br</span> loop <span class="hljs-comment"># go to start of loop	</span>

	<span class="hljs-title function_">end_loop:</span> 

<span class="hljs-keyword">.pos </span><span class="hljs-number">0x2000</span>
	<span class="hljs-title function_">i:</span>      <span class="hljs-keyword">.long </span><span class="hljs-number">0</span>
</code></pre>
              </div>
            </div></p>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Program Counter
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>The program counter is a special <a href="./Register">register</a> that <a href="./Memory Address">memory address</a> of the next <a href="./Machine Instructions">instruction</a> to be executed, it is continually incremented after an <a href="./Machine Instructions">instruction</a> is fetched. Control transfers, like <a href="./Jump Instruction">jumping</a> or <a href="./Branching Instruction">branching</a> can change the program counter in ways other than the standard basic incrementation.</p>
<p>When a <a href="./Procedure">subroutine</a> is called it <a href="./Branching Instruction">branches</a> as well as storing the preceding contents of the <a href="./Program Counter">program counter</a> somewhere, so that when it returns the saved contents of the program counter can be placed back into the program counter which can then resume sequential execution after the <a href="./Procedure">subroutine</a> call.</p>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Procedure
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>A procedure is the higher level generalization of a <a href="./Subroutine">subroutine</a> with its own <strong>name</strong>, <strong>arguments</strong> and <strong>local scope</strong>. Procedures can be <strong>called</strong> which causes their encased code to be run, and possibly a result bound when the function returns.</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">int</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">fib</span><span class="hljs-params">(n)</span> {
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (n == <span class="hljs-number">0</span> || n == <span class="hljs-number">1</span>) <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> n;

	<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> fib(n<span class="hljs-number">-1</span>) + fib(n<span class="hljs-number">-2</span>);
}
</code></pre><blockquote>
<p>Example of a procedure that returns the nth value of the Fibonacci <a href="./Sequence">sequence</a> in <a href="./C">C</a>.</p>
</blockquote>
<h1>Low Level Implementation</h1>
<h2><a href="./Call Stack">Call Stack</a></h2>
<p>Procedures can be implemented using a <a href="./Call Stack">call stack</a> to store and retrieve required information about the procedure such as the return address and any arguments.</p>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Call Stack
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>The <strong>call stack</strong> is a specific implementation of a <a href="./Stack">stack</a> which stores relevant information for a <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a> to execute.</p>
<p>The <strong>call stack</strong> is typically at the highest <a href="./Memory Address">memory address</a> possible for a given <a href="./Program">program</a> and then grows downwards (to lower <a href="./Memory Address">memory addresses</a>) towards the <a href="./Heap Memory">heap</a>.</p>
<h1>Stack Frame</h1>
<p>Each time a <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a> is called a new entry is created (called a &quot;stack frame&quot;). Each <strong>stack frame</strong> stores <a href="./Local Variable">local variables</a> of the <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a>, the <strong>return address</strong> and any <strong>arguments</strong> passed to the <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a>.</p>
<p>Additionally, the <strong>stack frame</strong> might include saved <a href="./Register">registers</a> if the <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a> calls another <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a>. When a <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a> is called usually the start of this <strong>stack frame</strong> is written to a common <a href="./Register">register</a> before invocation.</p>
<h2>Allocation</h2>
<p>When a new <strong>stack frame</strong> is allocated, space is reserved on the <strong>call stack</strong> for all data the <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a> needs during its execution. This process typically involves:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Adjusting the Stack Pointer:</strong> The stack pointer <a href="./Register">register</a> is moved (decremented) to allocate enough space for the new frame.</li>
<li><strong>Saving the Return Address:</strong> The <a href="./Memory Address">address</a> of the next instruction (the point where the <a href="./Program">program</a> should continue after the <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a> returns) is pushed onto the <a href="./Stack">stack</a>.</li>
<li><strong>Saving the Old Frame Pointer:</strong> The previous <strong>frame pointer</strong> is pushed onto the <a href="./Stack">stack</a> so it can be restored when returning.</li>
<li><strong>Setting the New Frame Pointer:</strong> The <strong>frame pointer</strong> is updated to the current top of the <a href="./Stack">stack</a>, marking the base of the new frame. This allows <a href="./Local Variable">local variables</a> and parameters to be accessed using fixed offsets.</li>
<li><strong>Allocating Space for Local Variables:</strong> The <a href="./Compiler">compiler</a> reserves space for all <a href="./Local Variable">local variables</a> defined within the <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a>.</li>
<li><strong>Saving Registers (Optional):</strong> If the <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a> will call other <a href="./Procedure">procedures</a> or use certain <a href="./Register">registers</a>, it may save the current <a href="./Register">register</a> values in the <strong>stack frame</strong> to preserve their state.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Deallocation</h2>
<p>When a <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a> finishes executing, its <strong>stack frame</strong> must be removed from the <strong>call stack</strong> so control can return to the calling <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a>. This process, known as <strong>stack frame deallocation</strong> or <strong>stack unwinding</strong>, typically involves the following steps:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Restoring Saved Registers (if any):</strong> Any <a href="./Register">registers</a> saved at the beginning of the <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a> are restored to their previous values to ensure the caller's state is unchanged.</li>
<li><strong>Releasing Local Variable Space:</strong> The <strong>stack pointer</strong> is adjusted (incremented) to free the <a href="./Memory">memory</a> that was used for <a href="./Local Variable">local variables</a> and temporary data.</li>
<li><strong>Restoring the Old Frame Pointer:</strong> The previously saved <strong>frame pointer</strong> is popped from the <a href="./Stack">stack</a>, restoring the caller's frame context.</li>
<li><strong>Returning to the Caller:</strong> The <strong>return address</strong> is popped from the <a href="./Stack">stack</a>, and control is transferred back to that <a href="./Memory Address">address</a>, resuming execution in the calling <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a>.</li>
</ul>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Dynamic Control Flow
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p><strong>Dynamic control flow</strong> refers to <a href="./Control Flow">control flow</a> where the target of a jump or call is determined at runtime rather than at compile time. This contrasts with <strong>static control flow</strong>, where the <a href="./Compiler">compiler</a> knows the exact destination address at compile time.</p>
<h1>Types of Dynamic Control Flow</h1>
<h2>Function Pointers</h2>
<p><a href="./Function Pointer">Function pointers</a> allow <a href="./Procedure">procedures</a> to be called indirectly by storing procedure addresses in variables and jumping to those addresses at runtime.</p>
<h2>Polymorphic Dispatch</h2>
<p>In <a href="./Object Oriented">object-oriented</a> languages like <a href="./Java">Java</a>, <a href="./Method">method</a> calls on objects use <a href="./Polymorphism">polymorphic dispatch</a> to determine which implementation to call based on the object's actual type at runtime.</p>
<h2>Jump Tables</h2>
<p><a href="./Jump Table">Jump tables</a> enable efficient implementation of multi-way branches, such as <code>switch</code> statements, by storing destination addresses in an array indexed by the condition value.</p>
<h1>Implementation</h1>
<p>Dynamic control flow requires:</p>
<ul>
<li>A way to store procedure/label addresses (as data)</li>
<li><a href="./Indirect Jump Instruction">indirect jump instructions</a> that can jump to an address stored in a <a href="./Register">register</a> or <a href="./Memory">memory</a></li>
</ul>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Function Pointer
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>A <strong>function pointer</strong> is a variable that stores the <a href="./Memory Address">address</a> of a <a href="./Procedure">procedure</a>. Function pointers enable <a href="./Dynamic Control Flow">dynamic control flow</a> by allowing the target of a procedure call to be determined at runtime.</p>
<h1>Declaration in C</h1>
<pre><code>&lt;<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span>-type&gt; (*&lt;var-name&gt;)(&lt;argument-<span class="hljs-built_in">list</span>&gt;);
</code></pre><h1>Example</h1>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">ping</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {
    <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;ping\n&quot;</span>);
}

<span class="hljs-type">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">foo</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {
    <span class="hljs-type">void</span> (*aFunc)();    <span class="hljs-comment">// Declare function pointer</span>
    aFunc = ping;       <span class="hljs-comment">// Assign function address</span>
    aFunc();            <span class="hljs-comment">// Call through pointer (calls ping)</span>
}
</code></pre><h1>Applications</h1>
<p>Function pointers enable several important programming patterns:</p>
<h2>Polymorphism</h2>
<p>In <a href="./C">C</a>, function pointers can implement <a href="./Polymorphism">polymorphic</a> behavior similar to <a href="./Object Oriented">object-oriented</a> languages:</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-class"><span class="hljs-keyword">struct</span> <span class="hljs-title">Animal</span> {</span>
    <span class="hljs-type">void</span> (*makeSound)(<span class="hljs-type">void</span>*);
};
</code></pre><h2>Generic Functions</h2>
<p>Function pointers allow writing <a href="./Generic Programming">generic</a> functions that can perform arbitrary operations:</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">map</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-type">int</span> (*fn)(<span class="hljs-type">int</span>, <span class="hljs-type">int</span>), <span class="hljs-type">int</span> n, <span class="hljs-type">int</span> *a, <span class="hljs-type">int</span> *b, <span class="hljs-type">int</span> *result)</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (<span class="hljs-type">int</span> i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt; n; i++)
        result[i] = fn(a[i], b[i]);
}
</code></pre><h2>Callbacks</h2>
<p>Function pointers enable <a href="./Event-Driven Programming">event-driven programming</a> by registering handlers to be called later:</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">diskRead</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-type">char</span>* buf, <span class="hljs-type">int</span> blockNum, <span class="hljs-type">int</span> numBytes, 
              <span class="hljs-type">void</span> (*whenComplete)(<span class="hljs-type">char</span>*, <span class="hljs-type">int</span>, <span class="hljs-type">int</span>))</span>;
</code></pre>
              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Polymorphism
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p><strong>Polymorphism</strong> is the ability of different types of objects to respond to the same <a href="./Method">method</a> call in different ways. In <a href="./Object Oriented">object-oriented</a> programming, polymorphism allows a single interface to represent different underlying forms (data types).</p>
<h1>Types of Polymorphism</h1>
<h2>Subtype Polymorphism (Runtime Polymorphism)</h2>
<p>The most common form in <a href="./Object Oriented">OOP</a>, where a variable of a parent type can refer to objects of any subtype, and method calls are dispatched to the appropriate implementation based on the object's actual type at runtime.</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Animal</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">makeSound</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> { System.out.println(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Some sound&quot;</span>); }
}

<span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Dog</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">extends</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Animal</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">makeSound</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> { System.out.println(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Bark&quot;</span>); }
}

<span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Cat</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">extends</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Animal</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">makeSound</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> { System.out.println(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Meow&quot;</span>); }
}

<span class="hljs-type">Animal</span> <span class="hljs-variable">a</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Dog</span>();
a.makeSound();  <span class="hljs-comment">// Prints &quot;Bark&quot; (not &quot;Some sound&quot;)</span>
</code></pre><h1>Polymorphic Dispatch</h1>
<p><strong>Polymorphic dispatch</strong> (also called <strong>dynamic dispatch</strong>) is the mechanism that determines which <a href="./Method">method</a> implementation to call at runtime:</p>
<ol>
<li>The variable has a static <strong>apparent type</strong> (e.g., <code>Animal</code>)</li>
<li>The object has a <a href="./Dynamic Control Flow">dynamic</a> <strong>actual type</strong> (e.g., <code>Dog</code>)</li>
<li>The actual type must be a subtype of the apparent type</li>
<li>Method calls invoke the actual type's implementation</li>
</ol>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Jump Table
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>A <strong>jump table</strong> is an array of <a href="./Memory Address">addresses</a> that enables efficient multi-way branching. Jump tables are commonly used to implement <code>switch</code> statements by indexing into the table based on the condition value and jumping to the corresponding address.</p>
<h1>Structure</h1>
<p>A jump table is simply an array where each element stores the address of a code label:</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">void</span> *jt[<span class="hljs-number">4</span>] = { &amp;&amp;L0, &amp;&amp;L1, &amp;&amp;L2, &amp;&amp;L3 };
</code></pre><p>In <a href="./SM213 Assembly">SM213 Assembly</a>:</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-title function_">jmptable:</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">.long </span>case0    <span class="hljs-comment"># Address of case 0</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">.long </span>case1    <span class="hljs-comment"># Address of case 1</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">.long </span>case2    <span class="hljs-comment"># Address of case 2</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">.long </span>default  <span class="hljs-comment"># Address of default</span>
</code></pre><h1>Switch Statement Implementation</h1>
<h2>C Code</h2>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-keyword">switch</span> (i) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span>: j = <span class="hljs-number">10</span>; <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-number">1</span>: j = <span class="hljs-number">11</span>; <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-number">2</span>: j = <span class="hljs-number">12</span>; <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">default</span>: j = <span class="hljs-number">14</span>; <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
}
</code></pre><h2>With Goto and Jump Table</h2>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">static</span> <span class="hljs-type">const</span> <span class="hljs-type">void</span>* jt[<span class="hljs-number">3</span>] = { &amp;&amp;L0, &amp;&amp;L1, &amp;&amp;L2 };
<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (i &lt; <span class="hljs-number">0</span> || i &gt; <span class="hljs-number">2</span>) <span class="hljs-keyword">goto</span> DEFAULT;
<span class="hljs-keyword">goto</span> *jt[i];

L0: j = <span class="hljs-number">10</span>; <span class="hljs-keyword">goto</span> CONT;
L1: j = <span class="hljs-number">11</span>; <span class="hljs-keyword">goto</span> CONT;
L2: j = <span class="hljs-number">12</span>; <span class="hljs-keyword">goto</span> CONT;
DEFAULT: j = <span class="hljs-number">14</span>;
CONT:
</code></pre><h2>In Assembly</h2>
<pre><code>    <span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> <span class="hljs-variable">$i</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>           <span class="hljs-comment"># r0 = &amp;i</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> (<span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>), <span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>         <span class="hljs-comment"># r0 = i</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> $<span class="hljs-number">-3</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>          <span class="hljs-comment"># r1 = -3</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">add</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>          <span class="hljs-comment"># r1 = i - 3</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">bgt</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>, default     <span class="hljs-comment"># if i &gt; 2, goto default</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> <span class="hljs-variable">$i</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>           <span class="hljs-comment"># r0 = i (reload)</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">beq</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>, default     <span class="hljs-comment"># if i &lt; 0, goto default</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> <span class="hljs-variable">$jmptable</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>    <span class="hljs-comment"># r1 = &amp;jmptable</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">j</span> *(<span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>)      <span class="hljs-comment"># Jump to jmptable[i]</span>
</code></pre><h1>Handling Gaps and Offsets</h1>
<h2>Gaps in case Labels</h2>
<p>If case labels have gaps, the jump table includes the <code>default</code> address for missing cases:</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-keyword">switch</span> (i) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-number">20</span>: j = <span class="hljs-number">10</span>; <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-number">21</span>: j = <span class="hljs-number">11</span>; <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-number">23</span>: j = <span class="hljs-number">13</span>; <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;  <span class="hljs-comment">// Note: case 22 missing</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">default</span>: j = <span class="hljs-number">14</span>; <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
}
</code></pre><p>Jump table for cases 20-23:</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">void</span> *jt[<span class="hljs-number">4</span>] = { &amp;&amp;L20, &amp;&amp;L21, &amp;&amp;DEFAULT, &amp;&amp;L23 };
<span class="hljs-keyword">goto</span> *jt[i - <span class="hljs-number">20</span>];  <span class="hljs-comment">// Normalize to 0-based index</span>
</code></pre><h2>Normalization</h2>
<p>Case labels are normalized by subtracting the minimum case value:</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (i &lt; <span class="hljs-number">20</span> || i &gt; <span class="hljs-number">23</span>) <span class="hljs-keyword">goto</span> DEFAULT;
<span class="hljs-keyword">goto</span> *jt[i - <span class="hljs-number">20</span>];  <span class="hljs-comment">// Maps 20→0, 21→1, 22→2, 23→3</span>
</code></pre><h1>Performance Tradeoffs</h1>
<h2>Jump Table Advantages</h2>
<ul>
<li><strong>Constant time</strong>: O(1) lookup regardless of number of cases</li>
<li><strong>Efficient for dense cases</strong>: When case values are close together</li>
</ul>
<h2>Jump Table Disadvantages</h2>
<ul>
<li><strong>Space overhead</strong>: Requires memory for all values in range</li>
<li><strong>Inefficient for sparse cases</strong>: Wastes space for missing values</li>
</ul>
<h2>When to Use</h2>
<p>The <a href="./Compiler">compiler</a> chooses between jump tables and <a href="./Conditional (Computer Science)">if-else chains</a> based on:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Scenario</th>
<th>Best Approach</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Dense cases (few gaps)</td>
<td>Jump table</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sparse cases (many gaps)</td>
<td>If-else chain</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Few cases (< 4-5)</td>
<td>If-else chain</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Large range (e.g., 1000-9000)</td>
<td>If-else chain</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Moderate range with most values</td>
<td>Jump table</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Switch Statement
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>A <strong>switch statement</strong> is a multi-way branch <a href="./Control Flow">control flow</a> construct that selects one of many code blocks to execute based on the value of an expression. Switch statements provide a more readable and potentially more efficient alternative to long chains of <a href="./Conditional (Computer Science)">if-else statements</a>.</p>
<h1>Syntax in C</h1>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-keyword">switch</span> (expression) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> constant1:
        <span class="hljs-comment">// code block 1</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> constant2:
        <span class="hljs-comment">// code block 2</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">default</span>:
        <span class="hljs-comment">// default code block</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
}
</code></pre><h1>Restrictions</h1>
<p>Switch statements have specific restrictions that enable efficient implementation:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Case labels must be constants</strong>: Values must be known at compile time</li>
<li><strong>Cardinal types only</strong>: Case values must be integers or characters (until <a href="./Java">Java</a> 1.7, which added strings)</li>
<li><strong>Equality comparison</strong>: Only tests equality, not ranges or complex conditions</li>
<li><strong>Single expression</strong>: All cases test the same expression</li>
</ul>
<p>These restrictions allow the <a href="./Compiler">compiler</a> to implement switches using <a href="./Jump Table">jump tables</a> for efficient O(1) branching.</p>
<h1>Implementation Strategies</h1>
<h2>If-Else Chain</h2>
<p>For sparse cases or few options, the compiler uses sequential comparisons:</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (i == <span class="hljs-number">20</span>) {
    j = <span class="hljs-number">10</span>;
} <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (i == <span class="hljs-number">21</span>) {
    j = <span class="hljs-number">11</span>;
} <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (i == <span class="hljs-number">42</span>) {
    j = <span class="hljs-number">12</span>;
} <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
    j = <span class="hljs-number">14</span>;
}
</code></pre><h2>Jump Table</h2>
<p>For dense cases, the compiler uses a <a href="./Jump Table">jump table</a>:</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-comment">// Original switch</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">switch</span> (i) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-number">20</span>: j = <span class="hljs-number">10</span>; <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-number">21</span>: j = <span class="hljs-number">11</span>; <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-number">22</span>: j = <span class="hljs-number">12</span>; <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">default</span>: j = <span class="hljs-number">14</span>; <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// Equivalent with jump table</span>
<span class="hljs-type">void</span> *jt[<span class="hljs-number">3</span>] = { &amp;&amp;L20, &amp;&amp;L21, &amp;&amp;L22 };
<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (i &lt; <span class="hljs-number">20</span> || i &gt; <span class="hljs-number">22</span>) <span class="hljs-keyword">goto</span> DEFAULT;
<span class="hljs-keyword">goto</span> *jt[i - <span class="hljs-number">20</span>];

L20: j = <span class="hljs-number">10</span>; <span class="hljs-keyword">goto</span> CONT;
L21: j = <span class="hljs-number">11</span>; <span class="hljs-keyword">goto</span> CONT;
L22: j = <span class="hljs-number">12</span>; <span class="hljs-keyword">goto</span> CONT;
DEFAULT: j = <span class="hljs-number">14</span>;
CONT:
</code></pre><h1>Assembly Implementation</h1>
<p>In <a href="./SM213 Assembly">SM213 Assembly</a>, jump tables enable efficient switches:</p>
<pre><code>    <span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> <span class="hljs-variable">$i</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>           <span class="hljs-comment"># r0 = &amp;i</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> (<span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>), <span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>         <span class="hljs-comment"># r0 = i</span>
    
    <span class="hljs-comment"># Check bounds: if i &lt; 20 or i &gt; 22, goto default</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> $<span class="hljs-number">-20</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">add</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>          <span class="hljs-comment"># r1 = i - 20</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> $<span class="hljs-number">0</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r2</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">bgt</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">r2</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>          <span class="hljs-comment"># if r1 &lt; 0 (i &lt; 20), goto default</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> $<span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r2</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">bgt</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r2</span>          <span class="hljs-comment"># if r1 &gt; 2 (i &gt; 22), goto default</span>
    
    <span class="hljs-comment"># Jump through table</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> <span class="hljs-variable">$jmptable</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r2</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">j</span> *(<span class="hljs-built_in">r2</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>)      <span class="hljs-comment"># jmptable[i - 20]</span>

<span class="hljs-title function_">case20:</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> $<span class="hljs-number">10</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">br</span> done
<span class="hljs-title function_">case21:</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> $<span class="hljs-number">11</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">br</span> done
<span class="hljs-title function_">case22:</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> $<span class="hljs-number">12</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">br</span> done
<span class="hljs-title function_">default:</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> $<span class="hljs-number">14</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">br</span> done

<span class="hljs-title function_">done:</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">ld</span> <span class="hljs-variable">$j</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">st</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">r1</span>, (<span class="hljs-built_in">r0</span>)

<span class="hljs-title function_">jmptable:</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">.long </span>case20
    <span class="hljs-keyword">.long </span>case21
    <span class="hljs-keyword">.long </span>case22
</code></pre><h1>Compiler Optimization</h1>
<p>The <a href="./Compiler">compiler</a> chooses the implementation strategy based on:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Cases</th>
<th>Strategy</th>
<th>Reason</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Sparse (large gaps)</td>
<td>If-else chain</td>
<td>Jump table would waste memory</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Few cases (<4-5)</td>
<td>If-else chain</td>
<td>Simpler, similar performance</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Dense (small gaps)</td>
<td>Jump table</td>
<td>O(1) lookup, worth the space</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Large range</td>
<td>If-else chain</td>
<td>Jump table too large</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h1>Fall-through Behavior</h1>
<p>Without <code>break</code>, execution continues to the next case:</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-keyword">switch</span> (i) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-number">1</span>:
        <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;One &quot;</span>);
        <span class="hljs-comment">// falls through</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-number">2</span>:
        <span class="hljs-built_in">printf</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;or Two\n&quot;</span>);
        <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
}
</code></pre><p>This is rarely desired and often causes bugs, which is why <a href="./Compiler">compilers</a> warn about missing <code>break</code> statements.</p>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Generic Programming
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p><strong>Generic programming</strong> is a programming paradigm where algorithms and data structures are written in terms of types that are specified later, allowing the same code to work with different data types. Generic code increases code reuse and reduces duplication.</p>
<h1>In C Using Function Pointers</h1>
<p><a href="./C">C</a> achieves generic programming through <a href="./Function Pointer">function pointers</a> and <code>void*</code> pointers, allowing functions to operate on any data type:</p>
<h2>Generic Iteration</h2>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">map</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-type">int</span> (*fn)(<span class="hljs-type">int</span>, <span class="hljs-type">int</span>), <span class="hljs-type">int</span> n, <span class="hljs-type">int</span> *s0, <span class="hljs-type">int</span> *s1, <span class="hljs-type">int</span> *dest)</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (<span class="hljs-type">int</span> i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt; n; i++)
        dest[i] = fn(s0[i], s1[i]);
}

<span class="hljs-type">int</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">add</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-type">int</span> a, <span class="hljs-type">int</span> b)</span> { <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> a + b; }
<span class="hljs-type">int</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">mul</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-type">int</span> a, <span class="hljs-type">int</span> b)</span> { <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> a * b; }

<span class="hljs-built_in">map</span>(add, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, array1, array2, result);  <span class="hljs-comment">// Add arrays</span>
<span class="hljs-built_in">map</span>(mul, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, array1, array2, result);  <span class="hljs-comment">// Multiply arrays</span>
</code></pre><h2>Generic Sorting</h2>
<p>The <a href="./C">C</a> standard library's <code>qsort</code> function is fully generic:</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-type">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">qsort</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-type">void</span> *base, <span class="hljs-type">size_t</span> nel, <span class="hljs-type">size_t</span> width,
           <span class="hljs-type">int</span> (*compare)(<span class="hljs-type">const</span> <span class="hljs-type">void</span>*, <span class="hljs-type">const</span> <span class="hljs-type">void</span>*))</span>;
</code></pre><p>Usage examples:</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-comment">// Sort integers</span>
<span class="hljs-type">int</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">cmpInt</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-type">const</span> <span class="hljs-type">void</span> *a, <span class="hljs-type">const</span> <span class="hljs-type">void</span> *b)</span> {
    <span class="hljs-type">int</span> ia = *(<span class="hljs-type">int</span>*)a;
    <span class="hljs-type">int</span> ib = *(<span class="hljs-type">int</span>*)b;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> ia - ib;
}
qsort(intArray, n, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(<span class="hljs-type">int</span>), cmpInt);

<span class="hljs-comment">// Sort strings</span>
<span class="hljs-type">int</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">cmpString</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-type">const</span> <span class="hljs-type">void</span> *a, <span class="hljs-type">const</span> <span class="hljs-type">void</span> *b)</span> {
    <span class="hljs-type">char</span> *sa = *(<span class="hljs-type">char</span>**)a;
    <span class="hljs-type">char</span> *sb = *(<span class="hljs-type">char</span>**)b;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">strcmp</span>(sa, sb);
}
qsort(strArray, n, <span class="hljs-keyword">sizeof</span>(<span class="hljs-type">char</span>*), cmpString);
</code></pre><h1>Using typedef for Clarity</h1>
<p>The <code>typedef</code> statement creates type aliases that make generic code more readable:</p>
<pre><code><span class="hljs-keyword">typedef</span> <span class="hljs-type">void</span>* <span class="hljs-type">element_t</span>;

<span class="hljs-type">int</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">partition</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-type">element_t</span>* <span class="hljs-built_in">array</span>, <span class="hljs-type">int</span> left, <span class="hljs-type">int</span> right, 
              <span class="hljs-type">int</span> (*cmp)(<span class="hljs-type">element_t</span>, <span class="hljs-type">element_t</span>))</span> {
    <span class="hljs-type">element_t</span> pivotValue, t;
    <span class="hljs-comment">// ... implementation</span>
}
